   And TRANSFLAG   < '2'                   

Update SLA_LabMaster                       
   Set JStatus = '2'                       
 Where SPECIMENNUM  = '2011260230'  
   AND OrderCode    = '2015'    
   AND Receiptdate = '2020-11-26'    
   And JStatus < '3'
